namespace = schaos

# Non tribal holding flies off in the sky
province_event = {
	id = schaos.1
	desc = EVTDESCschaos1
	picture = GFX_evt_chaos_hordes

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 5
	}

	trigger = {
		capital_scope = {
			region = world_chaos_wastes
			is_tribal = no
			is_nomadic = no
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos1
		convert_to = NOMAD
	}
}

# Building gets eaten by mouth in the ground
province_event = {
	id = schaos.2
	desc = EVTDESCschaos2
	picture = GFX_evt_chaos_hordes

	trigger = {
		capital_scope = {
			region = world_chaos_wastes
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1200
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos2
		destroy_random_building = yes
	}
}

# A band of Kurgan comes to offer services
character_event = {
	id = schaos.3
	desc = EVTDESCschaos3
	picture = GFX_evt_chaos_hordes
	min_age = 16
	#max_age = 250
	capable_only = yes
	only_rulers = yes
	prisoner = no
	religion_group = chaos_gods_group

	trigger = {
		capital_scope = {
			region = world_chaos_wastes
			OR = {
				is_tribal = yes
				is_nomadic = yes
			}
		}
		piety = 200
		war = yes
		trait = creature_human
		NOT = {
			trait = incapable
		}
		NOT = {
			trait = infirm
		}
		age = 16
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 900
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.95
			piety = 250
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			piety = 450
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			piety = 750
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			piety = 1000
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.95
			prestige = 500
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			prestige = 750
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			prestige = 1000
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			prestige = 1500
		}

	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos3
		location = {
			ROOT = {
				spawn_unit = {
					cannot_inherit = yes
					province = PREV
					owner = ROOT
					troops = {
						light_infantry = {
							250 250
						}
						heavy_infantry = {
							200 200
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Ruler wakes up with legged eye staring at him, it pees and runs away
character_event = {
	id = schaos.4
	desc = EVTDESCschaos4
	picture = GFX_evt_chaos_hordes
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes

	trigger = {
		location = {
			empire = {
				title = e_chaos_wastes
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 430
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos4
		hidden_tooltip = {
			change_variable = {
				which = "lunatic_counter" value = 2
			}
			character_event = {
				id = mutation.1005
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
							which = "khorne_favor" value = 1
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
							which = "nurgle_favor" value = 1
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
							which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 1
						}
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = {
							which = "khorne_favor" value = 1
						}
						check_variable = {
							which = "nurgle_favor" value = 1
						}
						check_variable = {
							which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 1
						}
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = "khorne_favor" value = -1
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = "nurgle_favor" value = -1
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = "slaanesh_favor" value = -1
				}
			}

		}
	}
}

# Reversed gravity
province_event = {
	id = schaos.5
	desc = EVTDESCschaos5
	picture = GFX_evt_chaos_hordes

	trigger = {
		empire = {
			title = e_chaos_wastes
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1250
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos5
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = reversed_gravity
			duration = 3600
		}
	}
}

# Hellgate opens
province_event = {
	id = schaos.6
	desc = EVTDESCschaos6
	picture = GFX_evt_chaos_hordes

	trigger = {
		empire = {
			title = e_chaos_wastes
		}
		NOT = {
			has_province_modifier = warphole_epicentre
		}
		any_neighbor_province = {
			NOT = {
				has_province_modifier = warphole_epicentre
			}
			any_neighbor_province = {
				NOT = {
					has_province_modifier = warphole_epicentre
				}
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 5950
	}

	immediate = {
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					religion = tzeentch
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 2
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					religion = slaanesh
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 2
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					religion = khorne
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = "khorne_favor" value = 2
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					religion = nurgle
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = "nurgle_favor" value = 2
				}
			}
		}

	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos6
		hidden_tooltip = {
			province_event = {
				id = schaos.8 days = 25 random = 40
			} # the eye strikes
			province_event = {
				id = schaos.7 days = 250 random = 900
			} # remove it
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = warphole_epicentre
				duration = -1
			}
			any_neighbor_province = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = warphole_epicentre
					duration = -1
				}
				province_event = {
					id = schaos.8 days = 25 random = 40
				} # the eye strikes
				province_event = {
					id = schaos.7 days = 250 random = 900
				} # remove it

			}

		}
	}
}

# Hellgate closes
province_event = {
	id = schaos.7
	hide_window = yes

	trigger = {
		has_province_modifier = warphole_epicentre
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		remove_province_modifier = warphole_epicentre
	}
}

# The Eye strikes - Disabled for now
province_event = {
	id = schaos.8
	desc = EVTDESCschaos8
	picture = GFX_evt_chaos_hordes
	notification = yes

	trigger = {
		has_province_modifier = warphole_epicentre
		always = no
	} 				# Disabled for now
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		province_event = {
			id = schaos.8 days = 25 random = 40
		}
		siege = {
			troops = -0.25
		}
		siege = {
			enemy = {
				morale = -0.1
				troops = -0.25
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos8
	}
}

# explosion of pus
character_event = {
	id = schaos.9
	desc = EVTDESCschaos9
	picture = GFX_evt_chaos_hordes

	trigger = {
		location = {
			region = world_chaos_wastes
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 4950
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos9
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
							which = "khorne_favor" value = 1
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
							which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 1
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
							which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 1
						}
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = "nurgle_favor" value = 1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = {
							which = "khorne_favor" value = 1
						}
						check_variable = {
							which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 1
						}
						check_variable = {
							which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 1
						}
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = "khorne_favor" value = -1
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = "tzeentch_favor" value = -1
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = "slaanesh_favor" value = -1
				}
			}
			character_event = {
				id = mutation.1005
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_dlc = "Reapers"
					}
				}
				random_list = {
					20 = {
						add_trait = has_nurgles_rot
					}
					20 = {
						add_trait = has_tuberculosis
					}
					20 = {
						add_trait = has_typhus
					}
					20 = {
						add_trait = has_bubonic_plague
					}
					20 = {
						add_trait = leper
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "Reapers"
				}
				add_symptom_effect = yes
			}
			any_courtier = {
				limit = {
					is_ruler = no
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							check_variable = {
								which = "khorne_favor" value = 1
							}
						}
						NOT = {
							check_variable = {
								which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 1
							}
						}
						NOT = {
							check_variable = {
								which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 1
							}
						}
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = "nurgle_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							check_variable = {
								which = "khorne_favor" value = 1
							}
							check_variable = {
								which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 1
							}
							check_variable = {
								which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 1
							}
						}
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = "khorne_favor" value = -1
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = "tzeentch_favor" value = -1
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = "slaanesh_favor" value = -1
					}
				}
				random_list = {
					20 = {
						add_trait = has_nurgles_rot
					}
					20 = {
						add_trait = has_tuberculosis
					}
					20 = {
						add_trait = has_typhus
					}
					20 = {
						add_trait = has_bubonic_plague
					}
					20 = {
						add_trait = leper
					}
				}

			}

		}
	}
}

# garden of delights
character_event = {
	id = schaos.10
	desc = EVTDESCschaos10
	picture = GFX_evt_chaos_hordes

	trigger = {
		location = {
			region = world_chaos_wastes
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 4950
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos10
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
							which = "khorne_favor" value = 1
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
							which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 1
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
							which = "nurgle_favor" value = 1
						}
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = {
							which = "khorne_favor" value = 1
						}
						check_variable = {
							which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 1
						}
						check_variable = {
							which = "nurgle_favor" value = 1
						}
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = "khorne_favor" value = -1
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = "tzeentch_favor" value = -1
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = "nurgle_favor" value = -1
				}
			}
			character_event = {
				id = mutation.1005
			}
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					add_trait = lustful
				}
				25 = {
					add_trait = gluttonous
				}
				25 = {
					add_trait = drunkard
				}
				25 = {
					add_trait = slothful
				}
			}
			any_courtier = {
				limit = {
					is_ruler = no
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							check_variable = {
								which = "khorne_favor" value = 1
							}
						}
						NOT = {
							check_variable = {
								which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 1
							}
						}
						NOT = {
							check_variable = {
								which = "nurgle_favor" value = 1
							}
						}
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							check_variable = {
								which = "khorne_favor" value = 1
							}
							check_variable = {
								which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 1
							}
							check_variable = {
								which = "nurgle_favor" value = 1
							}
						}
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = "khorne_favor" value = -1
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = "tzeentch_favor" value = -1
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = "nurgle_favor" value = -1
					}
				}
				random_list = {
					25 = {
						add_trait = lustful
					}
					25 = {
						add_trait = gluttonous
					}
					25 = {
						add_trait = drunkard
					}
					25 = {
						add_trait = slothful
					}
				}

			}

		}
	}
}

# blood river
province_event = {
	id = schaos.11
	desc = EVTDESCschaos11
	picture = GFX_evt_chaos_hordes

	trigger = {
		location = {
			region = world_chaos_wastes
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 3950
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos11
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
							which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 1
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
							which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 1
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
							which = "nurgle_favor" value = 1
						}
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = "khorne_favor" value = 1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = {
							which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 1
						}
						check_variable = {
							which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 1
						}
						check_variable = {
							which = "nurgle_favor" value = 1
						}
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = "slaanesh_favor" value = -1
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = "tzeentch_favor" value = -1
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = "nurgle_favor" value = -1
				}
			}
			character_event = {
				id = mutation.1005
			}
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					add_trait = wroth
				}
				25 = {
					add_trait = cruel
				}
				25 = {
					add_trait = ambitious
				}
				25 = {

							}
						}
						NOT = {
							check_variable = {
								which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 1
							}
						}
						NOT = {
							check_variable = {
								which = "nurgle_favor" value = 1
							}
						}
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = "khorne_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							check_variable = {
								which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 1
							}
							check_variable = {
								which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 1
							}
							check_variable = {
								which = "nurgle_favor" value = 1
							}
						}
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = "slaanesh_favor" value = -1
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = "tzeentch_favor" value = -1
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = "nurgle_favor" value = -1
					}
				}
				random_list = {

						add_trait = wroth

# living shadows
character_event = {
	id = schaos.12
	desc = EVTDESCschaos12
	picture = GFX_evt_chaos_hordes

	trigger = {
		location = {
			region = world_chaos_wastes
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 3950
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos12
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
							which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 1
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
							which = "khorne_favor" value = 1
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
							which = "nurgle_favor" value = 1
						}
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = {
							which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 1
						}
						check_variable = {
							which = "khorne_favor" value = 1
						}
						check_variable = {
							which = "nurgle_favor" value = 1
						}
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = "slaanesh_favor" value = -1
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = "khorne_favor" value = -1
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = "nurgle_favor" value = -1
				}
			}
			character_event = {
				id = mutation.1005
			}
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					add_trait = paranoid
				}
				25 = {
					add_trait = deceitful
				}
				25 = {
					add_trait = ambitious
				}
				25 = {
					add_trait = greedy
				}
			}
			any_courtier = {
				limit = {
					is_ruler = no
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							check_variable = {
								which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 1
							}
						}
						NOT = {
							check_variable = {
								which = "khorne_favor" value = 1
							}
						}

							check_variable = {
								which = "nurgle_favor" value = 1
							}
						}
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							check_variable = {
								which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 1
							}
							check_variable = {
								which = "khorne_favor" value = 1
							}
							check_variable = {
								which = "nurgle_favor" value = 1
							}
						}
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = "slaanesh_favor" value = -1
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = "khorne_favor" value = -1
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = "nurgle_favor" value = -1
					}
				}
				random_list = {
					25 = {
						add_trait = paranoid
					}
					25 = {
						add_trait = deceitful
					}
					25 = {
						add_trait = ambitious

				title = e_chaos_wastes
			}
		}
	}

		months = 450
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			NOT = {
				religion_group = chaos_gods_group
			}
		}
	}

			troops = -0.05
		}

				morale = -0.1
				troops = -0.05
			}
		}

# Visions of Chaos make leading commanders go insane (mostly for foreigners).
character_event = {
	id = schaos.16
	desc = EVTDESCschaos16
	picture = GFX_evt_chaos_hordes
	notification = yes

	trigger = {
		location = {
			empire = {
				title = e_chaos_wastes
			}
		}
		siege = {
			is_attacker = yes
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 350
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			NOT = {
				religion_group = chaos_gods_group
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		siege = {
			troops = -0.15
		}
		siege = {
			enemy = {
				morale = -0.1
				troops = -0.025
				leader = {
					any_liege = {
						limit = {
							war_with = ROOT
							NOT = {
								ROOT = {
									liege = {
										has_landed_title = e_rebels
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		random = {
			chance = 50
			add_trait = blinded
		}
		tooltip = {
			siege = {
				troops = -0.05
			}
			siege = {
				enemy = {
					morale = 0.1
					troops = -0.025
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos16
	}
}

# Failure - Prisoner escapes
character_event = {
	id = schaos.17005
	desc = EVTDESCschaos17005
	picture = GFX_evt_demon_summoning
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos17005
		prisoner = no
		random_independent_ruler = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = ROOT
			}
			ROOT = {
				move_character = PREV
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = schaos.17006
			}
		}
	}
}

# Prisoner has escaped, notify summoner
character_event = {
	id = schaos.17006
	desc = EVTDESCschaos17006
	picture = GFX_evt_demon_summoning
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos17006
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_quest = quest_chaos_cult_demonic_possession
				quest_target = {
					character = FROM
				}
			}
			clr_quest = {
				id = quest_chaos_cult_demonic_possession
				failure = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

# Failure - Prisoner explodes
character_event = {
	id = schaos.18
	desc = EVTDESCschaos18
	picture = GFX_evt_demon_summoning
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos18
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = schaos.18005
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_invincible_trigger = yes
			}
			antideath_effect = yes
			break = yes
		}
		death = {
			death_reason = death_execution
			killer = FROM
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				any_vassal = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							religion = cadai
							religion = asrai_cadai
							religion_group = old_world_group
						}
					}
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_evil_sorcerer
						who = FROM
					}
				} 
			} 
			any_dynasty_member = {
				limit = {
					religion_group = cytharai_group
				}
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_destroyed_family
					who = FROM
				}
			} 
			any_dynasty_member = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						religion_group = cytharai_group
					}
				}
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_destroyed_family
					who = FROM
				}
			} 
		} 
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = schaos.19
	desc = EVTDESCschaos19
	picture = GFX_evt_demon_summoning
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos19
		abdicate = yes
		hidden_tooltip = {
			set_graphical_culture = flamer_tzeentch
			culture = flamer_tzeentch
			religion = tzeentch
			remove_trait = kind
			remove_trait = content
			remove_trait = humble
			remove_trait = temperate
			remove_trait = slothful
			remove_trait = charitable
			remove_trait = infirm
			remove_trait = incapable
			remove_trait = wounded
			remove_trait = blinded
			remove_trait = idiot
			remove_trait = imbecile
			remove_trait = dim
			remove_trait = dumb
			remove_trait = bright
			remove_trait = brilliant
			remove_trait = quick
			remove_trait = witch_hunter
			remove_trait = on_witch_hunt
			remove_trait = has_nurgles_rot
			remove_trait = creature_human
			remove_trait = creature_dwarf
			remove_trait = creature_chaos_dwarf
			remove_trait = creature_elf
			remove_trait = creature_amazon
			remove_trait = creature_beastman
			add_trait = ambitious
			add_trait = proud
			add_trait = greedy
			add_trait = genius
			add_trait = tzeentch_demon
			add_trait = tzeentch_flamer
			set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_conversion
			set_character_flag = special_marshal
			health = 25
			any_lover = {
				remove_lover = ROOT
			}
			any_friend = {
				remove_friend = ROOT
			}
			any_spouse = {
				remove_spouse = ROOT
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						intrigue = 20
					}
				}
				change_intrigue = 15

			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						learning = 20
					}
				}
				change_learning = 15

			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					martial = 15
				}
				change_martial = -7

			}
		}
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = schaos.19005
			}
		}
		random_independent_ruler = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = ROOT
			}
			ROOT = {
				move_character = PREV
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				any_vassal = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							religion = cadai
							religion = asrai_cadai
							religion_group = old_world_group
						}
					}
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_evil_sorcerer
						who = FROM
					}
				} 
			} 
			any_dynasty_member = {
				limit = {
					religion_group = cytharai_group
				}
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_destroyed_family
					who = FROM
				}
			} 
			any_dynasty_member = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						religion_group = cytharai_group
					}
				}
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_destroyed_family
					who = FROM
				}
			} 
		} 
	}
}

# Failure - Flamer escapes - Notify summoner
character_event = {
	id = schaos.19005
	desc = EVTDESCschaos19005
	picture = GFX_evt_demon_summoning
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos19005
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_quest = quest_chaos_cult_demonic_possession
				quest_target = {
					character = FROM
				}
			}
			clr_quest = {
				id = quest_chaos_cult_demonic_possession
				failure = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

# Success - Flamer summoned
character_event = {
	id = schaos.20
	desc = EVTDESCschaos20
	picture = GFX_evt_demon_summoning
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos20
		abdicate = yes
		move_character = FROM
		hidden_tooltip = {
 		 	1 = {
				change_variable = {
					which = "doom_counter" value = 1
				}
			}
			set_graphical_culture = flamer_tzeentch
			culture = flamer_tzeentch
			religion = tzeentch
			remove_trait = kind
			remove_trait = content
			remove_trait = humble
			remove_trait = temperate
			remove_trait = slothful
			remove_trait = charitable
			remove_trait = infirm
			remove_trait = incapable
			remove_trait = wounded
			remove_trait = blinded
			remove_trait = idiot
			remove_trait = imbecile
			remove_trait = dim
			remove_trait = dumb
			remove_trait = bright
			remove_trait = brilliant
			remove_trait = quick
			remove_trait = witch_hunter
			remove_trait = on_witch_hunt
			remove_trait = has_nurgles_rot
			remove_trait = creature_human
			remove_trait = creature_dwarf
			remove_trait = creature_chaos_dwarf
			remove_trait = creature_elf
			remove_trait = creature_amazon
			remove_trait = creature_beastman
			add_trait = ambitious
			add_trait = proud
			add_trait = greedy
			add_trait = genius
			add_trait = tzeentch_demon
			add_trait = tzeentch_flamer
			set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_conversion
			set_character_flag = special_marshal
			health = 25
			any_lover = {
				remove_lover = ROOT
			}
			any_friend = {
				remove_friend = ROOT
			}
			any_spouse = {
				remove_spouse = ROOT
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						intrigue = 20
					}
				}
				change_intrigue = 15

			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						learning = 20
					}
				}
				change_learning = 15

			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					martial = 15
				}
				change_martial = -7

			}
		}
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = schaos.20005
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				any_vassal = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							religion = cadai
							religion = asrai_cadai
							religion_group = old_world_group
						}
					}
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_evil_sorcerer
						who = FROM
					}
				} 
			} 
			any_dynasty_member = {
				limit = {
					religion_group = cytharai_group
				}
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_destroyed_family
					who = FROM
				}
			} 
			any_dynasty_member = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						religion_group = cytharai_group
					}
				}
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_destroyed_family
					who = FROM
				}
			} 
		} 
	}
}

# Success - Flamer summoned - Notify summoner
character_event = {
	id = schaos.20005
	desc = EVTDESCschaos20005
	picture = GFX_evt_demon_summoning
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos20005
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_quest = quest_chaos_cult_demonic_possession
				quest_target = {
					character = FROM
				}
			}
			clr_quest = quest_chaos_cult_demonic_possession
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						is_female = yes
					}
				}
				sound_effect = devil_worshippers_demonic_possession_female
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						is_female = no
					}
				}
				sound_effect = devil_worshippers_demonic_possession_male
			}
			add_society_currency_medium_effect = yes
		}
		add_friend = FROM
		prestige = 500
		FROM = {
			prisoner = no
		}
	}
}

# Failure - Plaguebearer escapes
character_event = {
	id = schaos.21
	desc = EVTDESCschaos21
	picture = GFX_evt_demon_summoning
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos21
		abdicate = yes
		hidden_tooltip = {
			set_graphical_culture = plaguebearer_nurgle
			culture = plaguebearer_nurgle
			religion = nurgle
			remove_trait = cruel
			remove_trait = ambitious
			remove_trait = proud
			remove_trait = gluttonous
			remove_trait = diligent
			remove_trait = greedy
			remove_trait = infirm
			remove_trait = incapable
			remove_trait = scarred
			remove_trait = idiot
			remove_trait = imbecile
			remove_trait = dim
			remove_trait = dumb
			remove_trait = bright
			remove_trait = brilliant
			remove_trait = quick
			remove_trait = witch_hunter
			remove_trait = on_witch_hunt
			remove_trait = creature_human
			remove_trait = creature_dwarf
			remove_trait = creature_chaos_dwarf
			remove_trait = creature_elf
			remove_trait = creature_amazon
			remove_trait = creature_beastman
			add_trait = content
			add_trait = humble
			add_trait = charitable
			add_trait = has_nurgles_rot
			add_trait = leper
			add_trait = nurgle_demon
			add_trait = nurgle_plaguebearer
			add_trait = ill
			set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_conversion
			set_character_flag = special_marshal
			health = 25
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					add_trait = has_tuberculosis
				}
				25 = {
					add_trait = has_typhoid_fever
				}
				25 = {
					add_trait = has_bubonic_plague
				}
				25 = {
					add_trait = has_measles
				}

			}
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					add_trait = has_small_pox
				}
				25 = {
					add_trait = syphilitic
				}
				25 = {
					add_trait = pneumonic
				}
				25 = {
					add_trait = has_typhus
				}

			}
			any_lover = {
				remove_lover = ROOT
			}
			any_friend = {
				remove_friend = ROOT
			}
			any_spouse = {
				remove_spouse = ROOT
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						stewardship = 20
					}
				}
				change_stewardship = 15

			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						diplomacy = 20
					}
				}
				change_diplomacy = 15

			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					martial = 15
				}
				change_martial = -7

			}
		}
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = schaos.21005
			}
		}
		random_independent_ruler = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = ROOT
			}
			ROOT = {
				move_character = PREV
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				any_vassal = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							religion = cadai
							religion = asrai_cadai
							religion_group = old_world_group
						}
					}
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_evil_sorcerer
						who = FROM
					}
				} 
			} 
			any_dynasty_member = {
				limit = {
					religion_group = cytharai_group
				}
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_destroyed_family
					who = FROM
				}
			} 
			any_dynasty_member = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						religion_group = cytharai_group
					}
				}
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_destroyed_family
					who = FROM
				}
			} 
		} 
	}
}

	id = schaos.23
	desc = EVTDESCschaos23
	picture = GFX_evt_demon_summoning
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos23
		abdicate = yes
		hidden_tooltip = {
			set_graphical_culture = daemonette_slaanesh
			culture = daemonette_slaanesh
			religion = slaanesh
			remove_trait = kind
			remove_trait = chaste
			remove_trait = celibate
			remove_trait = content
			remove_trait = humble
			remove_trait = temperate
			remove_trait = diligent
			remove_trait = charitable
			remove_trait = infirm
			remove_trait = incapable
			remove_trait = wounded
			remove_trait = blinded

			remove_trait = imbecile

			remove_trait = creature_elf
			remove_trait = creature_amazon
			remove_trait = creature_beastman
			remove_trait = has_nurgles_rot
			remove_trait = ill
			add_trait = cruel
			add_trait = deceitful
			add_trait = slaanesh_demon
			add_trait = slaanesh_daemonette
			set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_conversion
			set_character_flag = special_marshal
			health = 25
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					add_trait = lustful
				}
				25 = {
					add_trait = greedy
				}
				25 = {
					add_trait = gluttonous
				}
				25 = {
					add_trait = slothful
				}
				25 = {
					add_trait = proud
				}
				25 = {
					add_trait = envious
				}

			}
			any_lover = {
				remove_lover = ROOT
			}

			}

			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					stewardship = 15
				}
				change_stewardship = -7

			}
		}
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = schaos.23005
			}
		}
		random_independent_ruler = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = ROOT
			}
			ROOT = {
				move_character = PREV
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {

			remove_trait = content

			remove_trait = diligent

			remove_trait = creature_chaos_dwarf
			remove_trait = creature_elf

			remove_trait = ill
			add_trait = cruel
			add_trait = deceitful
			add_trait = slaanesh_demon
			add_trait = slaanesh_daemonette

			set_character_flag = special_marshal

				25 = {
					add_trait = lustful
				}
				25 = {
					add_trait = greedy
				}

				}
				25 = {
					add_trait = slothful
				}
				25 = {
					add_trait = proud
				}
				25 = {
					add_trait = envious
				}

			}
			any_lover = {
				remove_lover = ROOT
			}
			any_friend = {
				remove_friend = ROOT
			}
			any_spouse = {
				remove_spouse = ROOT
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						intrigue = 20
					}
				}
				change_intrigue = 15

			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						diplomacy = 20
					}
				}
				change_diplomacy = 15

			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					stewardship = 15
				}
				change_stewardship = -7

			}
		}
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = schaos.24005
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				any_vassal = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							religion = cadai
							religion = asrai_cadai
							religion_group = old_world_group
						}
					}
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_evil_sorcerer
						who = FROM
					}
				} 
			} 
			any_dynasty_member = {

				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_destroyed_family
					who = FROM
				}

character_event = {
	id = schaos.24005
	desc = EVTDESCschaos24005
	picture = GFX_evt_demon_summoning
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos24005
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_quest = quest_chaos_cult_demonic_possession
				quest_target = {
					character = FROM
				}
			}
			clr_quest = quest_chaos_cult_demonic_possession
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						is_female = yes
					}
				}
				sound_effect = devil_worshippers_demonic_possession_female
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						is_female = no
					}
				}
				sound_effect = devil_worshippers_demonic_possession_male
			}
			add_society_currency_medium_effect = yes
		}
		add_friend = FROM
		prestige = 500
		FROM = {
			prisoner = no
		}
	}
}

					factor = 0.25
					has_character_modifier = magic_power_1
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					has_character_modifier = magic_power_2
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					has_character_modifier = magic_power_3
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.75
					has_character_modifier = magic_power_4
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.75
					trait = hedge_wizard
				}
				character_event = {
					id = DR_chaos_dwarf.52
				} # success, summoned khorne demon
			}
			50 = {
				character_event = {
					id = schaos.28
				}
			} # failure, demon drags you to the Warp

		}
	}
}

# CLEANUP EVENTS FOR DEMON COURTIERS

# Demons of different gods in the same court kill each other
character_event = {
	id = schaos.33
	desc = EVTDESCschaos33
	picture = GFX_evt_chaos_hordes
	min_age = 666
	religion_group = chaos_gods_group

	trigger = {
		ai = no
		OR = {
			AND = {
				trait = khorne_demon
				any_courtier = {
					ai = no
					OR = {
						trait = slaanesh_demon
						trait = nurgle_demon
						trait = tzeentch_demon
						trait = hashut_kdaai
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				trait = slaanesh_demon
				any_courtier = {
					ai = no
					OR = {
						trait = khorne_demon
						trait = nurgle_demon
						trait = tzeentch_demon
						trait = hashut_kdaai
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				trait = nurgle_demon
				any_courtier = {
					ai = no
					OR = {
						trait = khorne_demon
						trait = slaanesh_demon
						trait = tzeentch_demon
						trait = hashut_kdaai
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				trait = tzeentch_demon
				any_courtier = {
					ai = no
					OR = {
						trait = khorne_demon
						trait = slaanesh_demon
						trait = nurgle_demon
						trait = hashut_kdaai
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				trait = hashut_kdaai
				any_courtier = {
					ai = no
					OR = {
						trait = khorne_demon
						trait = slaanesh_demon
						trait = nurgle_demon
						trait = tzeentch_demon
					}
				}
			}

		}

	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos33
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				ai = no
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
				OR = {
					trait = khorne_demon
					trait = slaanesh_demon
					trait = nurgle_demon
					trait = tzeentch_demon
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_invincible_trigger = yes
				}
				antideath_effect = yes
				break = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
}

# on_death of cultist summoner, send back to the warp all his generic demons (not those summoned by the events above)
character_event = {
	id = schaos.36
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_character_flag = summonedkhornehost
			has_character_flag = summonednurglehost
			has_character_flag = summonedslaaneshhost
			has_character_flag = summonedtzeentchhost
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		any_friend = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = host_demon_commander
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_invincible_trigger = yes
				}
				antideath_effect = yes
				break = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_unknown
			}
		}
	}
}

# on_death of mage summoner, demons either passes down to the heir or disperses (not those summoned by the events above)
character_event = {
	id = schaos.37
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		any_friend = {
			OR = {
				trait = khorne_demon
				trait = nurgle_demon
				trait = slaanesh_demon
				trait = tzeentch_demon
			}
			NOR = {
				trait = prince_khorne
				trait = prince_nurgle
				trait = prince_slaanesh
				trait = prince_tzeentch
			}
			NOT = {
				has_character_flag = host_demon_commander
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ruler = yes
				current_heir = {
					dynasty = ROOT
				}
			}
			any_friend = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trait = khorne_demon
						trait = nurgle_demon
						trait = slaanesh_demon
						trait = tzeentch_demon
					}
					NOR = {
						trait = prince_khorne
						trait = prince_nurgle
						trait = prince_slaanesh
						trait = prince_tzeentch
					}
				}
				set_character_flag = inheriting_demon
				current_heir = {
					add_friend = PREV
					PREV = {
						move_character = THIS
					}
					character_event = {
						id = schaos.38 days = 1
					}
				}

			}
			break = yes
		}
		any_friend = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trait = khorne_demon
					trait = nurgle_demon
					trait = slaanesh_demon
					trait = tzeentch_demon
				}
				NOR = {
					trait = prince_khorne
					trait = prince_nurgle
					trait = prince_slaanesh
					trait = prince_tzeentch
				}
				NOT = {
					has_character_flag = inheriting_demon
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_invincible_trigger = yes
				}
				antideath_effect = yes
				break = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_unknown
			}
		}
	}
}

# A demon has come to you
character_event = {
	id = schaos.38
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCAschaos38
		trigger = {
			any_friend = {
				has_character_flag = inheriting_demon
				trait = khorne_demon
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCBschaos38
		trigger = {
			any_friend = {
				has_character_flag = inheriting_demon
				trait = nurgle_demon
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCCschaos38
		trigger = {
			any_friend = {
				has_character_flag = inheriting_demon
				trait = slaanesh_demon
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCDschaos38
		trigger = {
			any_friend = {
				has_character_flag = inheriting_demon
				trait = tzeentch_demon
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_chaos_hordes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		# Accept services
		name = EVTOPTAschaos38
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					religion_group = chaos_gods_group
				}
			}
			piety = -500
		}
		any_friend = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trait = khorne_demon
					trait = nurgle_demon
					trait = slaanesh_demon
					trait = tzeentch_demon
				}
			}
			clr_character_flag = inheriting_demon
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					FROM = {
						religion = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.01
				any_friend = {
					count = 2
					OR = {
						trait = khorne_demon
						trait = nurgle_demon
						trait = slaanesh_demon
						trait = tzeentch_demon
					}
				}
			}

		}
	}

	option = {
		# Refuse services
		name = EVTOPTBschaos38
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = chaos_gods_group
			}
			piety = -150
		}
		any_friend = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trait = khorne_demon
					trait = nurgle_demon
					trait = slaanesh_demon
					trait = tzeentch_demon
				}
				has_character_flag = inheriting_demon
			}
			clr_character_flag = inheriting_demon
			remove_friend = ROOT
			banish = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				FROM = {
					religion = ROOT
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				any_friend = {
					count = 2
					OR = {
						trait = khorne_demon
						trait = nurgle_demon
						trait = slaanesh_demon
						trait = tzeentch_demon
					}
				}
			}

		}
	}
}

# A demon is roaming about with no familiar
character_event = {
	id = schaos.39
	hide_window = yes
	min_age = 666
	religion_group = chaos_gods_group

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 48
	}

	trigger = {
		is_ruler = no
		NOT = {
			num_of_friends = 1
		}
		OR = {
			trait = khorne_demon
			trait = nurgle_demon

			}
		}

					trait = khorne_demon

# witch hunter tries to kill the demon
character_event = {
	id = schaos.43
	title = DEMON_HUNT
	desc = EVTDESCschaos43
	picture = "GFX_evt_demon_fighting"
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos43
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROMFROM = {
				random_list = {
					40 = {
						modifier = {
							factor = 1.5
							learning = 15
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 1.75
							learning = 20
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 1.75
							learning = 25
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 1.75
							trait = scholarly_theologian
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 1.95
							trait = mastermind_theologian
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 0.75
							trait = dim
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 0.5
							trait = dumb
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 0.5
							trait = slow
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 0.25
							trait = idiot
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 0.25
							trait = imbecile
						}
						FROMFROM = {
							character_event = {
								id = schaos.46
							}
						} # demon dies

					}
					60 = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								is_invincible_trigger = yes
							}
							antideath_effect = yes
							break = yes
						}
						death = {
							death_reason = death_murder
							killer = FROMFROM
						}
						FROM = {
							character_event = {
								id = schaos.44
							}
						} # notify liege witch hunter died
						FROMFROM = {
							banish = yes
							random_friend = {
								remove_friend = FROMFROM
								character_event = {
									id = schaos.45
								}
							}
						}
					}

				}

			}
		}
	}
}

			piety = 150
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					num_of_friends = 1
				}
			}
			random_friend = {
				character_event = {
					id = schaos.47
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_invincible_trigger = yes
			}
			antideath_effect = yes
			break = yes
		}
		death = {
			death_reason = death_execution
			killer = FROM
		}
	}
}

							}
						}
						add_trait = hardy
					}
					character_event = {
						id = schaos.57
					}
					character_event = {
						id = mutation.1 days = 80 random = 120
					}
				}

			}

		}
	}

		piety = -75

character_event = {
	id = schaos.60
	desc = EVTDESCschaos60
	picture = "GFX_evt_slaanesh"
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		# More
		name = EVTOPTAschaos60
		random_list = {
			33 = {
				change_diplomacy = 1
				set_character_flag = slaanesh_cheating_dipl
			}
			33 = {
				change_intrigue = 1
				set_character_flag = slaanesh_cheating_intr
			}
			34 = {
			}

		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
 			# Slaanesh rigs the game, for your pleasure
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = slaanesh_cheating_dipl
				}
				change_diplomacy = -1
				clr_character_flag = slaanesh_cheating_dipl
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = slaanesh_cheating_intr
				}
				change_intrigue = -1
				clr_character_flag = slaanesh_cheating_intr
			}
			random_list = {
				15 = {
					change_diplomacy = 1
				}
				15 = {
					change_intrigue = 1
				}
				70 = {
					health = -1
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								health = 0
							}
							NOT = {
								has_artifact = carstein_ring
							}
							NOT = {
								trait = khemri_tomb_king
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								is_invincible_trigger = yes
							}
							antideath_effect = yes
							break = yes
						}
						death = {
							death_reason = death_murder_unknown
						}
						break = yes
					}
				}

			}
			character_event = {
				id = schaos.60
			}

		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
	}

	option = {
		# Stop
		name = EVTOPTBschaos60
		piety = -75
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
	}
}

# Slaaneshi forces full agnatic/enatic realm
character_event = {
	id = schaos.71
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCAschaos71
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					is_female = yes
					NOT = {
						trait = homosexual
					}
				}
				AND = {
					is_female = no
					trait = homosexual
				}

			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCBschaos71
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					is_female = no
					NOT = {
						trait = homosexual
					}
				}
				AND = {
					is_female = yes
					trait = homosexual
				}

			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_esorcism
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		trait = possessed
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos71
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						is_female = yes
						NOT = {
							trait = homosexual
						}
					}
					AND = {
						is_female = no
						trait = homosexual
					}

				}

			}
			any_demesne_title = {
				add_law = agnatic_succession
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						is_female = yes
						NOT = {
							trait = homosexual
						}
					}
					AND = {
						is_female = no
						trait = homosexual
					}

				}

			}
			any_demesne_title = {
				add_law = enatic_succession
			}
		}
		any_vassal = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_possessed_w
				who = ROOT
				years = 5
			}

				id = schaos.71005

					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.85
						trait = bright
					}
					modifier = {

					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.65
						trait = quick
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = brilliant
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.45
						trait = genius
					}
					modifier = {

				3 = {

						which = "possession_counter" value = -5

						learning = 30
					}

						factor = 1.5
						trait = genius
					}

# A Khornate mage? For shame. For shame!
long_character_event = {
	id = schaos.83
	desc = EVTDESCschaos83
	picture = GFX_evt_khorne
	min_age = 16
	capable_only = yes
	religion = khorne

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 20
	}

	trigger = {
		religion = khorne
		OR = {
			has_character_modifier = magic_power_1
			has_character_modifier = magic_power_2
			has_character_modifier = magic_power_3
			has_character_modifier = magic_power_4
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBschaos83
		piety = -150
		hidden_tooltip = {
			long_character_event = {
				id = schaos.83005
			}
		}
	}
}

# A Khornate mage? For shame. For shame! - Part 2
long_character_event = {
	id = schaos.83005
	desc = EVTDESCschaos83005
	picture = GFX_evt_khorne
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos83005
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trait = lore_nurgle
				 	trait = lore_slaanesh
				}
			}
			remove_trait = lore_nurgle
			remove_trait = lore_slaanesh
			add_trait = lore_tzeentch
		}
		piety = -750
		religion = tzeentch
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBschaos83005
		piety = -150
		hidden_tooltip = {
			remove_character_modifier = magic_power_1
			remove_character_modifier = magic_power_2
			remove_character_modifier = magic_power_3
			remove_character_modifier = magic_power_4
			clr_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_1
			clr_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_2
			clr_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_3
			clr_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_4
			clr_character_flag = recessive_mage
			remove_trait = magic_potential_1
			remove_trait = magic_potential_2
			remove_trait = magic_potential_3
			remove_trait = magic_potential_4
		}
	}
}

# Mage is asked to perform a demon summoning from liege

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos84

				chance = 20

					id = mutation.1 days = 100 random = 100
				}
			}

				name = magic_cooldown_summoning
				duration = 300
				hidden = yes
			}

				character_event = {
					id = schaos.86
				}
			}
		} # receive event and decide what to do
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				ROOT = {
					opinion = {
						who = FROM
						value = 20
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				ROOT = {
					opinion = {
						who = FROM
						value = 40
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				ROOT = {
					opinion = {
						who = FROM
						value = 60
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				ROOT = {
					opinion = {
						who = FROM
						value = 80
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.75
				ROOT = {
					opinion = {
						who = FROM
						value = 100
					}
				}
			}
		}

# Failure - Sucked in the Warp alongside the mage
character_event = {
	id = schaos.87
	desc = EVTDESCschaos87
	picture = GFX_evt_demon_summoning
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos87
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_invincible_trigger = yes
			}
			antideath_effect = yes
			break = yes
		}
		death = {
			death_reason = death_accident
		}
	}
}

# Prize of your chosing (army, strength, health)
character_event = {
	id = schaos.92001
	desc = EVTDESCschaos92001
	picture = GFX_evt_khorne
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
 		1 = {
			change_variable = {
				which = "doom_counter" value = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "nurgle_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = "khorne_favor" value = 4
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "nurgle_favor" value = 1
					}
					check_variable = {
						which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 1
					}
					check_variable = {
						which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = "nurgle_favor" value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 0
			}
		}

	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos92001
		capital_scope = {
			ROOT = {
				spawn_unit = {
					province = PREV
					home = PREV
					owner = THIS
					attrition = 0.5
					cannot_inherit = yes
					earmark = demonic_host
 					troops = {
						daemonic_host = {
							350 350
						}
					}
				}
				spawn_unit = {
					province = PREV
					home = PREV
					owner = THIS
					attrition = 0.5
					cannot_inherit = yes
					earmark = demonic_host
 					troops = {
						daemonic_host = {
							250 250
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBschaos92001
		change_martial = 2
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = tough
			}
			remove_trait = tough
			add_trait = strong
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = hardy
			}
			remove_trait = hardy
			add_trait = strong
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					trait = strong
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = tough
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = hardy
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = soft
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = fragile
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = weak
				}

			}
			add_trait = tough
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = soft
			}
			remove_trait = soft
			add_trait = tough
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = fragile
			}
			remove_trait = fragile
			add_trait = hardy
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = weak
			}
			remove_trait = weak
			add_trait = hardy
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTCschaos92001
		health = 8
	}
}

# Khorne sends Bloodletter
character_event = {
	id = schaos.92002
	desc = EVTDESCschaos92002
	picture = GFX_evt_khorne
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		1 = {
			change_variable = {
				which = "doom_counter" value = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "nurgle_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = "khorne_favor" value = 3
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "nurgle_favor" value = 1
					}
					check_variable = {
						which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 1
					}
					check_variable = {
						which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = "nurgle_favor" value = -5
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = "slaanesh_favor" value = -5
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = "tzeentch_favor" value = -5
			}
		}

	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos92002
		create_character = {
			random_traits = yes
			religion = khorne
			culture = bloodletter_khorne
			female = no
			age = 888
			flag = ai_flag_refuse_conversion
			flag = special_marshal
			attributes = {
				diplomacy = 10
				martial = 18
				stewardship = 2
				intrigue = 25
				learning = 9
			}
		}
		new_character = {
			add_trait = wroth
			add_trait = honest
			add_trait = khorne_demon
			add_trait = khorne_bloodletter
			health = 25
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					add_trait = ambitious
				}
				25 = {
					add_trait = gregarious
				}
				25 = {
					add_trait = diligent
				}
				25 = {
					add_trait = proud
				}

			}
			add_friend = ROOT
		}
		prestige = 500
	}
}

# Prize of your chosing (magic, love, presents)
character_event = {
	id = schaos.93001
	desc = EVTDESCschaos93001
	picture = GFX_evt_nurgle
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
 		1 = {
			change_variable = {
				which = "doom_counter" value = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "khorne_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = "nurgle_favor" value = 4
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "khorne_favor" value = 1
					}
					check_variable = {
						which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 1
					}
					check_variable = {
						which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = "khorne_favor" value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 0
			}
		}

	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos93001
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				trait = hedge_wizard
			}
			NOT = {
				trait = mage_apprentice
			}
			NOT = {
				has_character_modifier = magic_power_1
			}
			NOT = {
				has_character_modifier = magic_power_2
			}
			NOT = {
				has_character_modifier = magic_power_3
			}
			NOT = {
				has_character_modifier = magic_power_4
			}
		}
		add_trait = lore_nurgle
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_1
			}
			clr_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_1
			add_trait = magic_potential_1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_2
			}
			clr_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_2
			add_trait = magic_potential_2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_3
			}
			clr_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_3
			add_trait = magic_potential_3
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_4
			}
			clr_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_4
			add_trait = magic_potential_4
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					trait = magic_potential_1
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = magic_potential_2
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = magic_potential_3
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = magic_potential_4
				}
				NOT = {
					has_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_1
				}
				NOT = {
					has_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_2
				}
				NOT = {
					has_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_3
				}
				NOT = {
					has_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_4
				}
			}
			add_trait = magic_potential_2
		}
		z_magic_power_sequential_addition = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBschaos93001
		change_stewardship = 1
		any_vassal = {
			random = {
				chance = 75
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_loving_liege
					who = FROM
				}
			}

		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTCschaos93001
		any_vassal = {
			random = {
				chance = 50
				add_trait = has_nurgles_rot
			}

		}
	}
}

# Nurgle sends Plaguebearer
character_event = {
	id = schaos.93002
	desc = EVTDESCschaos93002
	picture = GFX_evt_nurgle
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		1 = {
			change_variable = {
				which = "doom_counter" value = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "khorne_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = "nurgle_favor" value = 3
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "khorne_favor" value = 1
					}
					check_variable = {
						which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 1
					}
					check_variable = {
						which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = "khorne_favor" value = -5
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = "slaanesh_favor" value = -5
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = "tzeentch_favor" value = -5
			}
		}

	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos93002
		create_character = {
			random_traits = yes
			religion = nurgle
			culture = plaguebearer_nurgle
			female = no
			age = 777
			flag = ai_flag_refuse_conversion
			flag = special_marshal
			attributes = {
				diplomacy = 8
				martial = 3
				stewardship = 32
				intrigue = 10
				learning = 12
			}
		}
		new_character = {
			add_trait = content
			add_trait = humble
			add_trait = charitable
			add_trait = has_nurgles_rot
			add_trait = leper
			add_trait = nurgle_demon
			add_trait = nurgle_plaguebearer
			add_trait = ill
			health = 25
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					add_trait = has_tuberculosis
				}
				25 = {
					add_trait = has_typhoid_fever
				}
				25 = {
					add_trait = has_bubonic_plague
				}
				25 = {
					add_trait = has_measles
				}

			}
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					add_trait = has_small_pox
				}
				25 = {
					add_trait = syphilitic
				}
				25 = {
					add_trait = pneumonic
				}
				25 = {
					add_trait = has_typhus
				}

			}
			add_friend = ROOT
		}
		prestige = 500
	}
}

# Prize of your chosing (magic, beauty, healing)
character_event = {
	id = schaos.94001
	desc = EVTDESCschaos94001
	picture = GFX_evt_slaanesh
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
 		1 = {
			change_variable = {
				which = "doom_counter" value = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "khorne_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "nurgle_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 4
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "khorne_favor" value = 1
					}
					check_variable = {
						which = "nurgle_favor" value = 1
					}
					check_variable = {
						which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = "khorne_favor" value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = "nurgle_favor" value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 0
			}
		}

	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos94001
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				trait = hedge_wizard
			}
			NOT = {
				trait = mage_apprentice
			}
			NOT = {
				has_character_modifier = magic_power_1
			}
			NOT = {
				has_character_modifier = magic_power_2
			}
			NOT = {
				has_character_modifier = magic_power_3
			}
			NOT = {
				has_character_modifier = magic_power_4
			}
		}
		add_trait = lore_slaanesh
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_1
			}
			clr_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_1
			add_trait = magic_potential_1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_2
			}
			clr_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_2
			add_trait = magic_potential_2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_3
			}
			clr_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_3
			add_trait = magic_potential_3
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_4
			}
			clr_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_4
			add_trait = magic_potential_4
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					trait = magic_potential_1
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = magic_potential_2
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = magic_potential_3
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = magic_potential_4
				}
				NOT = {
					has_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_1
				}
				NOT = {
					has_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_2
				}
				NOT = {
					has_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_3
				}
				NOT = {
					has_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_4
				}
			}
			add_trait = magic_potential_2
		}
		z_magic_power_sequential_addition = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBschaos94001
		change_intrigue = 1
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = pretty
			}
			remove_trait = pretty
			add_trait = beautiful
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = fair
			}
			remove_trait = fair
			add_trait = beautiful
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					trait = beautiful
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = pretty
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = fair
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = plain
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = ugly
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = unsightly
				}

			}
			add_trait = pretty
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = plain
			}
			remove_trait = plain
			add_trait = pretty
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = ugly
			}
			remove_trait = ugly
			add_trait = fair
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = unsightly
			}
			remove_trait = unsightly
			add_trait = fair
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTCschaos94001
		health = 5
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = wounded
			}
			remove_trait = wounded
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = maimed
			}
			remove_trait = maimed
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = blinded
			}
			remove_trait = blinded
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = eunuch
			}
			remove_trait = eunuch
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = incapable
			}
			remove_trait = incapable
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = disfigured
			}
			remove_trait = disfigured
		}
	}
}

# Slaanesh sends Daemonette
character_event = {
	id = schaos.94002
	desc = EVTDESCschaos94002
	picture = GFX_evt_slaanesh
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		1 = {
			change_variable = {
				which = "doom_counter" value = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "khorne_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "nurgle_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 3
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "khorne_favor" value = 1
					}
					check_variable = {
						which = "nurgle_favor" value = 1
					}
					check_variable = {
						which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = "khorne_favor" value = -5
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = "nurgle_favor" value = -5
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = "tzeentch_favor" value = -5
			}
		}

	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos94002
		create_character = {
			random_traits = yes
			religion = slaanesh
			culture = daemonette_slaanesh
			female = no
			age = 666
			flag = ai_flag_refuse_conversion
			flag = special_marshal
			attributes = {
				diplomacy = 20
				martial = 18
				stewardship = 2
				intrigue = 25
				learning = 9
			}
		}
		new_character = {
			add_trait = cruel
			add_trait = deceitful
			add_trait = slaanesh_demon
			add_trait = slaanesh_daemonette
			health = 25
			random_list = {
				34 = {
					add_trait = lustful
				}
				33 = {
					add_trait = greedy
				}
				33 = {
					add_trait = gluttonous
				}

			}
			random_list = {
				34 = {
					add_trait = slothful
				}
				33 = {
					add_trait = proud
				}
				33 = {
					add_trait = lustful
				}

			}
			add_friend = ROOT
		}
		prestige = 500
	}
}

# Slaanesh bestows upon you a gift of flesh
character_event = {
	id = schaos.94007
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "khorne_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "nurgle_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "khorne_favor" value = 1
					}
					check_variable = {
						which = "nurgle_favor" value = 1
					}
					check_variable = {
						which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 1
					}

# Prize of your chosing (magic, beauty, healing)
character_event = {
	id = schaos.95001
	desc = EVTDESCschaos95001
	picture = GFX_evt_tzeentch
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
 		1 = {
			change_variable = {
				which = "doom_counter" value = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "khorne_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "nurgle_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 4
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "khorne_favor" value = 1
					}
					check_variable = {
						which = "nurgle_favor" value = 1
					}
					check_variable = {
						which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = "khorne_favor" value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = "nurgle_favor" value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 0
			}
		}

	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos95001
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				trait = hedge_wizard
			}
			NOT = {
				trait = mage_apprentice
			}
			NOT = {
				has_character_modifier = magic_power_1
			}
			NOT = {
				has_character_modifier = magic_power_2
			}
			NOT = {
				has_character_modifier = magic_power_3
			}
			NOT = {
				has_character_modifier = magic_power_4
			}
		}
		add_trait = lore_tzeentch
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_1
			}
			clr_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_1
			add_trait = magic_potential_1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_2
			}
			clr_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_2
			add_trait = magic_potential_2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_3
			}
			clr_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_3
			add_trait = magic_potential_3
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_4
			}
			clr_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_4
			add_trait = magic_potential_4
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					trait = magic_potential_1
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = magic_potential_2
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = magic_potential_3
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = magic_potential_4
				}
				NOT = {
					has_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_1
				}
				NOT = {
					has_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_2
				}
				NOT = {
					has_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_3
				}
				NOT = {
					has_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_4
				}
			}
			add_trait = magic_potential_2
		}
		z_magic_power_sequential_addition = yes
		z_magic_power_sequential_addition = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBschaos95001
		change_intrigue = 1
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = brilliant
			}
			remove_trait = brilliant
			add_trait = genius
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = quick
			}
			remove_trait = quick
			add_trait = genius
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = smart
			}
			remove_trait = smart
			add_trait = genius
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = bright
			}
			remove_trait = bright
			add_trait = brilliant
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					trait = genius
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = brilliant
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = quick
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = smart
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = bright
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = dim
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = dumb
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = slow
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = idiot
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = imbecile
				}

			}
			add_trait = brilliant
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = dim
			}
			remove_trait = dim
			add_trait = quick
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = dumb
			}
			remove_trait = dumb
			add_trait = quick
		}
		if = {

		if = {

# Tzeentch sends Flamer
character_event = {
	id = schaos.95002
	desc = EVTDESCschaos95002
	picture = GFX_evt_tzeentch
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		1 = {
			change_variable = {
				which = "doom_counter" value = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "khorne_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "nurgle_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 3
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "khorne_favor" value = 1
					}
					check_variable = {
						which = "nurgle_favor" value = 1
					}
					check_variable = {
						which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = "khorne_favor" value = -5
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = "nurgle_favor" value = -5
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = "slaanesh_favor" value = -5
			}
		}

	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos95002
		create_character = {
			random_traits = yes
			religion = tzeentch
			culture = flamer_tzeentch
			female = no
			age = 999
			attributes = {
				diplomacy = 2
				martial = 13
				stewardship = 2
				intrigue = 30
				learning = 18
			}
			trait = tzeentch_demon
			trait = tzeentch_flamer
			trait = ambitious
			trait = proud
			trait = greedy
			health = 25
			flag = ai_flag_refuse_conversion
			flag = special_marshal
		}
		new_character = {
			add_friend = ROOT
		}
		prestige = 500
	}
}

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "khorne_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "nurgle_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "khorne_favor" value = 1
					}
					check_variable = {
						which = "nurgle_favor" value = 1
					}
					check_variable = {
						which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = "khorne_favor" value = -4
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = "nurgle_favor" value = -4
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = "slaanesh_favor" value = -4
			}
		}

	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos95003
		add_trait = lore_tzeentch
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_1
			}
			clr_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_1
			add_trait = magic_potential_1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_2
			}
			clr_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_2
			add_trait = magic_potential_2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_3
			}
			clr_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_3
			add_trait = magic_potential_3
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_4
			}
			clr_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_4
			add_trait = magic_potential_4
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					trait = magic_potential_1
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = magic_potential_2
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = magic_potential_3
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = magic_potential_4
				}
				NOT = {
					has_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_1
				}
				NOT = {
					has_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_2
				}
				NOT = {
					has_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_3
				}
				NOT = {
					has_character_flag = magic_potential_flag_4
				}
			}
			add_trait = magic_potential_2
		}
		z_magic_power_sequential_addition = yes
		prestige = 250
	}
}

# Tzeentch shows a sign of his favor
character_event = {
	id = schaos.95004
	desc = EVTDESCschaos95004
	picture = GFX_evt_tzeentch
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		1 = {
			change_variable = {
				which = "doom_counter" value = 2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "khorne_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "nurgle_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 7
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "khorne_favor" value = 1
					}
					check_variable = {
						which = "nurgle_favor" value = 1
					}
					check_variable = {
						which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = "khorne_favor" value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = "nurgle_favor" value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 0
			}
		}

	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos95004
		piety = 350
	}
}

# Becoming a Champion
character_event = {
	id = schaos.97
	desc = EVTDESCschaos97
	picture = "GFX_evt_chosen_kurgan"
	religion_group = chaos_gods_group
	capable_only = yes
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 100

	trigger = {
		trait = creature_human
		prestige = 150
		piety = 150
		NOT = {
			has_nickname = nick_the_forsaken
		}
		NOT = {
			trait = champion_khorne
		}
		NOT = {
			trait = champion_nurgle
		}
		NOT = {
			trait = champion_slaanesh
		}
		NOT = {
			trait = champion_tzeentch
		}
		NOT = {
			trait = chosen_khorne
		}
		NOT = {
			trait = chosen_nurgle
		}
		NOT = {
			trait = chosen_slaanesh
		}
		NOT = {
			trait = chosen_tzeentch
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = khorne
				NOT = {
					trait = craven
				}
				NOT = {
					has_character_modifier = magic_power_1
				}
				NOT = {
					has_character_modifier = magic_power_2
				}
				NOT = {
					has_character_modifier = magic_power_3
				}
				NOT = {
					has_character_modifier = magic_power_4
				}
				check_variable = {
					which = "khorne_favor" value = 10
				}
			}
			AND = {
				religion = nurgle
				NOT = {
					trait = greedy
				}
				check_variable = {
					which = "nurgle_favor" value = 10
				}
			}
			AND = {
				religion = slaanesh
				NOT = {
					trait = chaste
				}
				check_variable = {
					which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 10
				}
			}
			AND = {
				religion = tzeentch
				NOT = {
					trait = content
				}
				check_variable = {
					which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 10
				}
			}
			AND = {
				religion = chaos
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "khorne_favor" value = 10
					}
					check_variable = {
						which = "nurgle_favor" value = 10
					}
					check_variable = {
						which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 10
					}
					check_variable = {
						which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 10
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 120
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			piety = 500
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			piety = 1000
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			piety = 1500
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			piety = 2000
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			OR = {
				check_variable = {
					which = "khorne_favor" value = 15
				}
				check_variable = {
					which = "nurgle_favor" value = 15
				}
				check_variable = {
					which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 15
				}
				check_variable = {
					which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 15
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			OR = {
				check_variable = {
					which = "khorne_favor" value = 25
				}
				check_variable = {
					which = "nurgle_favor" value = 25
				}
				check_variable = {
					which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 25
				}
				check_variable = {
					which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 25
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			OR = {
				check_variable = {
					which = "khorne_favor" value = 35
				}
				check_variable = {
					which = "nurgle_favor" value = 35
				}
				check_variable = {
					which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 35
				}
				check_variable = {
					which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 35
				}
			}
		}

	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAschaos97
		prestige = 500
		piety = 250
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = khorne
			}
			add_trait = champion_khorne
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = nurgle
			}
			add_trait = champion_nurgle
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = slaanesh
			}
			add_trait = champion_slaanesh
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = tzeentch
			}
			add_trait = champion_tzeentch
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = chaos
			}
			random_list = {
				# Undivided
				30 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 5
						check_variable = {
							which = "khorne_favor" value = 5
						}
						check_variable = {
							which = "nurgle_favor" value = 5
						}
						check_variable = {
							which = "slaanesh_favor" value = 5
						}
						check_variable = {
							which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 5
						}
					}

						factor = 5
						check_variable = {
							which = "khorne_favor" value = 10
						}
						check_variable = {
							which = "nurgle_favor" value = 10
						}
						check_variable = {

						}
						check_variable = {
							which = "tzeentch_favor" value = 10
						}

					add_trait = champion_undivided
				}
				# Khorne
				20 = {

						}
					}
					modifier = {

						check_variable = {
							which = "khorne_favor" value = 35
						}
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 20
						any_friend = {
							trait = khorne_demon
						}
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 10
						OR = {
							trait = strong
							trait = tough
							trait = hardy
							trait = duelist
							trait = brave
							trait = khorne_berserker

						}
					}
					add_trait = champion_khorne
				}
				# Nurgle
				20 = {

						}
					}
					modifier = {

							which = "nurgle_favor" value = 35
						}
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 20

							trait = nurgle_demon
						}
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 10
						OR = {
							trait = kind
							trait = charitable
							trait = humble
							trait = content
							is_ill = yes

						}
					}
					add_trait = champion_nurgle
				}
				# Tzeentch
